<td><span id="MIDL2369"></span><span id="midl2369"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1476"><dt><strong>MIDL2369</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1476"><dt><strong>MIDL2369</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1477"><dt><span id="exceeded_stack_size_for__Oi__using__Os"></span><span id="exceeded_stack_size_for__oi__using__os"></span><span id="EXCEEDED_STACK_SIZE_FOR__OI__USING__OS"></span>se ha superado el tamaño de pila para/OI, mediante/os</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1477"><dt><span id="exceeded_stack_size_for__Oi__using__Os"></span><span id="exceeded_stack_size_for__oi__using__os"></span><span id="EXCEEDED_STACK_SIZE_FOR__OI__USING__OS"></span>exceeded stack size for /Oi, using /Os</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1478">El modo de optimización-OI está limitado a 128 bytes de espacio de pila para los parámetros.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1478">The -Oi optimization mode is limited to 128 bytes of stack space for parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1479">El compilador ha cambiado automáticamente al modo de optimización del sistema operativo para evitar esta limitación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1479">The compiler has automatically switched to the Os optimization mode to work around this limitation.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1480">Para evitar esta advertencia, use los modos de optimización-Oicf o-os.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1480">To avoid this warning, use the -Oicf or -Os optimization modes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1481">El modo de optimización se puede cambiar en la línea de comandos especificando-Oicf o-os en lugar de-OI o agregando un atributo [optimize9 &quot; ICF &quot; )] u optimizar [( &quot; s &quot; )] a la función en el archivo ACF.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1481">The optimization mode may be changed on the command line by specifying -Oicf or -Os instead of -Oi or by adding an [optimize9&quot;icf&quot;)] or optimize[(&quot;s&quot;)] attribute to the function in the ACF file.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1482">Normalmente, esta advertencia se produce al pasar estructuras grandes como parámetros por valor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1482">This warning typically happens when passing large structures as parameters by value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1483">Se puede reducir el tamaño de pila necesario pasando un puntero a la estructura en su lugar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1483">The required stack size can be lowered by passing a pointer to the structure instead.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1484">Ejemplo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1484">Example:</span></span><br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>typedef struct
{
char a[127];
}
large;
//This function has a stack size of 132 (x86) or 136 (alpha) on 32-bit systems
void roo(large s, int a);    //MIDL 2360
// workaround: pass by reference
void bar (large *s, int a);</code></pre>
</dd> </dl></td>
</tr>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1643"><dt><span id="internal_compiler_inconsistency_detected__the_format_string_offset_is_invalid._See_the_documentation_for_more_information."></span><span id="internal_compiler_inconsistency_detected__the_format_string_offset_is_invalid._see_the_documentation_for_more_information."></span><span id="INTERNAL_COMPILER_INCONSISTENCY_DETECTED__THE_FORMAT_STRING_OFFSET_IS_INVALID._SEE_THE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_MORE_INFORMATION."></span>incoherencia interna del compilador detectada: el desplazamiento de la cadena de formato no es válido. <td><span id="MIDL2414"></span><span id="midl2414"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1669"><dt><strong>MIDL2414</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1669"><dt><strong>MIDL2414</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1670"><dt><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-Oicf__using_-OI"></span><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-oicf__using_-oi"></span><span id="FLOATING_POINT_OR_COMPLEX_RETURN_TYPES_WITH__DECODE__ARE_NOT_SUPPORTED_IN_-OICF__USING_-OI"></span>no se admiten tipos de valor devueltos de punto flotante o complejos con [descode] en-Oicf, mediante-OI</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1670"><dt><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-Oicf__using_-OI"></span><span id="floating_point_or_complex_return_types_with__decode__are_not_supported_in_-oicf__using_-oi"></span><span id="FLOATING_POINT_OR_COMPLEX_RETURN_TYPES_WITH__DECODE__ARE_NOT_SUPPORTED_IN_-OICF__USING_-OI"></span>floating point or complex return types with [decode] are not supported in -Oicf, using -OI</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1671">Los procedimientos con tipos de valor devueltos de punto flotante o de estructura/Unión no se admiten en la selección del estilo-Oicf.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1671">Procedures with floating point or structure/union return types are not supported in the -Oicf style pickling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1672">Una solución alternativa para 32 bits es usar el modo de optimización-OI al serializar datos (mediante [encode] y/o [descode]).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1672">A work around for 32-bit is to use the -Oi optimization mode when serializing data (using [encode] and/or [decode]).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1673">Sin embargo, como el intérprete de estilo anterior OI y la compatibilidad con la selección están preparadas para salirse de la versión 2000 de Windows, se recomienda encarecidamente usar punteros como solución alternativa para este problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1673">However, as the old -Oi style interpreter and pickling support are slated to be phased out after the Windows 2000 release, using pointers is strongly suggested as the work around for this problem.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1674">Tenga en cuenta también que, normalmente, el cambio de un método de interfaz para usar un puntero [out, ref] en lugar del valor devuelto que causa el problema es totalmente compatible con la conexión y se puede ocultar fácilmente desde la capa de la aplicación.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1674">Also note that typically, changing an interface method to use an [out, ref] pointer instead of the return value causing the problem is fully backward-compatible on wire and can be easily hidden from the app layer.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1675">Esta advertencia se puede suprimir globalmente especificando-OI en la línea de comandos de MIDL o para una función individual agregando el atributo [Optimize ( &quot; i &quot; )] a la función en el archivo ACF.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1675">This warning can be suppressed globally by specifying -Oi on the MIDL command line or for an individual function by adding the [optimize(&quot;i&quot;)] attribute to the function in the ACF file.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1676">En el ejemplo siguiente se muestra el problema:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1676">The following example demonstrates the issue:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1677">Roo. idl:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1677">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>double GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1678">Roo. ACF:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1678">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1679">Una opción para solucionar esta limitación sería pasar un parámetro [out] para que contenga el resultado en lugar de usar un valor devuelto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1679">One option to work around this limitation would be to pass an [out] parameter to hold the result instead of using a return value:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1680">Roo. idl:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1680">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>void GetDouble([out] double *result); //top level pointer is a [ref] pointer</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1681">Roo. ACF:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1681">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1682">Como se mencionó anteriormente, la solución que se ha descrito anteriormente es buena no solo para las nuevas interfaces, sino también como solución alternativa para los antiguos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1682">As mentioned earlier, the solution described above is good not only for the new interfaces but also as a work-around for the old ones.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1683">La representación de conexión para el &quot; nuevo &quot; argumento out es igual que para el valor devuelto (aviso void como nuevo valor devuelto).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1683">The wire representation for the new &quot;out&quot; argument is the same as for the return value (notice void as the new return value).</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1685"><dt><span id="the_return_type_is_not_supported_for_64-bit_when_using__decode_"></span><span id="THE_RETURN_TYPE_IS_NOT_SUPPORTED_FOR_64-BIT_WHEN_USING__DECODE_"></span>el tipo de valor devuelto no se admite para 64 bits al usar [descode]</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1685"><dt><span id="the_return_type_is_not_supported_for_64-bit_when_using__decode_"></span><span id="THE_RETURN_TYPE_IS_NOT_SUPPORTED_FOR_64-BIT_WHEN_USING__DECODE_"></span>the return type is not supported for 64-bit when using [decode]</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1686">Los procedimientos con tipos de valor devueltos de punto flotante o de mode when performing data serialization (using [ <a href="encode.md"><strong>encode</strong></a>] and/or [ <a href="decode.md"><strong>decode</strong></a>]).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1687">Está relacionado con el intérprete de estilo OI anterior y el serializador de datos no se admite en la plataforma de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1687">This is related to the old style -Oi interpreter and data serializer not being supported on 64-bit platform.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1688">Para obtener más información, consulte la descripción de MIDL2414.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1688">Please see the description of MIDL2414 for more information.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1689">En el ejemplo siguiente se muestra este error:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1689">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1690">Roo. idl:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1690">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>double GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1691">Roo. ACF:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1691">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1692">Lo siguiente se recomienda como solución alternativa para las interfaces nuevas y antiguas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1692">The following is advised as a work-around for both new and old interfaces.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1693">Use un parámetro [out] para almacenar el resultado en lugar de usar un valor devuelto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1693">Use an [out] parameter to hold the result instead of using a return value:</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1694">Roo. idl:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1694">roo.idl:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>void GetDouble([out] double *result); //top level pointer is a [ref] pointer.</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1695">Roo. ACF:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1695">roo.acf:</span></span> <br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>[decode] GetDouble();</code></pre>
<span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1696">Tenga en cuenta que esta solución es totalmente compatible con la conexión, ya que la representación de conexión de un puntero [Ref, out] o Double es igual que la de Double.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1696">Note that this solution is fully backward-compatible on wire, as the wire representation of a [ref, out] pointer or a double is the same as that of a double.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>

<td><span id="MIDL2416"></span><span id="midl2416"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1697"><dt><strong>MIDL2416</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1697"><dt><strong>MIDL2416</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1698"><dt><span id="transmitted_type_may_not_contain_a_full_pointer_for_either__wire_marshal__or__user_marshal_"></span><span id="TRANSMITTED_TYPE_MAY_NOT_CONTAIN_A_FULL_POINTER_FOR_EITHER__WIRE_MARSHAL__OR__USER_MARSHAL_"></span>el tipo transmitido no puede contener un puntero completo para [wire_marshal] o [user_marshal]</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1698"><dt><span id="transmitted_type_may_not_contain_a_full_pointer_for_either__wire_marshal__or__user_marshal_"></span><span id="TRANSMITTED_TYPE_MAY_NOT_CONTAIN_A_FULL_POINTER_FOR_EITHER__WIRE_MARSHAL__OR__USER_MARSHAL_"></span>transmitted type may not contain a full pointer for either [wire_marshal] or [user_marshal]</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1699">Los tipos con atributos [ <a href="wire-marshal.md"><strong>wire_marshal</strong></a>] o [ <a href="user-marshal.md"><strong>user_marshal</strong></a>] no pueden contener punteros completos ([ <strong>ptr</strong>]).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1699">Types with [ <a href="wire-marshal.md"><strong>wire_marshal</strong></a>] or [ <a href="user-marshal.md"><strong>user_marshal</strong></a>] attributes may not contain full ([ <strong>ptr</strong>]) pointers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1700">Use [ <a href="unique.md"><strong>Unique</strong></a>] o [ <a href="ref.md"><strong>ref</strong></a>] en su lugar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1700">Use [ <a href="unique.md"><strong>unique</strong></a>] or [ <a href="ref.md"><strong>ref</strong></a>] instead.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1701">En el ejemplo siguiente se muestra este error:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1701">The following example demonstrates this error:</span></span><br/>
<pre class="syntax" data-space="preserve"><code>typedef struct
{
    [ptr] long *a;    //Should use [ref] or [unique] instead
}
st1;
typedef [wire_marshal(st1)] struct
{
    long a;
}
st2:
void roo(st2 *s);    //MIDL2416</code></pre>
</dd> </dl></td>

st1;

<td><span id="MIDL9008"></span><span id="midl9008"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1721"><dt><strong>MIDL9008</strong></dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1721"><dt><strong>MIDL9008</strong></dt> </span></span></dl></td>
<td><dl> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1722"><dt><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._See_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._see_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_INTERNAL_COMPILER_PROBLEM__SYSTEM_ERROR_CODE__-_THE_COMPILER_CANNOT_CONTINUE_FOR_AN_UNKNOWN_REASON._SEE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_A_WORKAROUND."></span> problema interno del compilador <system error code> - el compilador no puede continuar por un motivo desconocido.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1722"><dt><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._See_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_internal_compiler_problem__system_error_code__-_the_compiler_cannot_continue_for_an_unknown_reason._see_documentation_for_a_workaround."></span><span id="_INTERNAL_COMPILER_PROBLEM__SYSTEM_ERROR_CODE__-_THE_COMPILER_CANNOT_CONTINUE_FOR_AN_UNKNOWN_REASON._SEE_DOCUMENTATION_FOR_A_WORKAROUND."></span> internal compiler problem <system error code> - the compiler cannot continue for an unknown reason.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1723">Consulte la documentación para obtener una solución alternativa.</dt> </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1723">See documentation for a workaround.</dt> </span></span><dd> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1724">El compilador no pudo continuar y se desconoce la causa del error.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1724">The compiler could not continue and the cause of the error is unknown.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1725">El número de error hexadecimal es un identificador de error del sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1725">The hexadecimal error number is a system-error identifier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1726">Puede que se haya producido un error en la compilación debido a un problema externo, como una condición de memoria insuficiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1726">The compile may have failed because of an external problem, such as an out-of-memory condition.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1727">En ese caso, puede encontrar más información en Winerror. h o NTSTATUS. h.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1727">In that case, you can find more information in Winerror.h or Ntstatus.h.</span></span> <br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1728">Hay dos situaciones en las que normalmente se genera este error:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1728">There are two situations that usually generate this error:</span></span><br/>
<ul>
<li><span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1729">No se pudo recuperar el compilador de MIDL tras detectar un error en el archivo IDL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1729">The MIDL compiler failed to recover after detecting an error in the IDL file.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1730">Si MIDL devolvió algún mensaje de error sobre el archivo IDL, intente corregirlos y volver a compilarlos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1730">If MIDL returned any error messages about your IDL file, try fixing them and recompiling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1731">Si no hay ningún mensaje de error, es posible que se haya producido un error en el compilador antes de que se pudiera informar de un error.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1731">If there are no error messages, the compiler may have failed before it could report an error.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1732">Busque un error de sintaxis en la línea para la que se notifique el error interno del compilador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1732">Look for a syntax error on the line for which the internal compiler error is reported.</span></span></li>
<li><span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1733">El compilador MIDL no pudo generar el código correcto con una opción de optimización especificada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1733">The MIDL compiler could not generate correct code under a specified optimization option.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1734">Intente cambiar los modos de compilador, compilar en optimización de modo mixto (/<a href="-os.md"><strong>os</strong></a>) o quitar todas las optimizaciones.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1734">Try changing compiler modes, compiling in mixed-mode optimization (/<a href="-os.md"><strong>Os</strong></a>), or removing all optimizations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1735">O bien, vuelva a compilar con la marca/NO_FORMAT_OPT para suprimir la optimización predeterminada del procedimiento y los descriptores de tipo de MIDL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1735">Or, recompile using the /NO_FORMAT_OPT flag to suppress MIDL's default optimization of procedure and type descriptors.</span></span></li>
</ul>
<span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1736">En ocasiones, este error se produce aunque el archivo IDL sea correcto y no se utilicen opciones de optimización.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1736">Occasionally this error occurs even when the IDL file is correct and no optimization options are being used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1737">Si este es el caso, intente volver a escribir la sección de código cerca de donde se comunicó el error quitando las modificaciones recientes, simplificando o reorganizando los tipos de datos, cambiando los prototipos o, de lo contrario, empiece a comentar partes del archivo IDL para localizar el código del problema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1737">If this is the case, try rewriting the section of code in the vicinity of where the error was reported by removing any recent modifications, simplifying or rearranging data types, changing prototypes, or else begin to comment out portions of the IDL file to locate the problem code.</span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="2e2cf-1738">Si ninguna de estas opciones funciona, o si cree que el problema puede estar relacionado con un error en Midl.exe, notifíquelo a Microsoft y proporcione todos los detalles pertinentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2e2cf-1738">If none of these options works, or if you think the problem may be related to a bug in Midl.exe, please notify Microsoft, giving all the relevant details.</span></span><br/> </dd> </dl></td>
</tr>
